┌───────────────────┐
│ PROBLEM STATEMENT │
└───────────────────┘
A carpet installer needs to efficiently cut rectangular carpet pieces from a single standard-sized roll, minimizing waste.

### Given:

- 1 standard carpet roll measuring 12ft × 50ft
- Need to cut the following rectangular pieces:
  1. 6ft × 8ft (quantity: 1)
  2. 4ft × 5ft (quantity: 1)
  3. 5ft × 7ft (quantity: 1)
  4. 8ft × 10ft (quantity: 1)

### Constraints:

1. All pieces must be placed without overlap
2. Pieces can optionally be rotated 90 degrees
3. All pieces must fit within the roll dimensions

### Objective:

Minimize the total length of carpet roll used



┌─────────────┐
│ FINAL MODEL │
└─────────────┘
0 | % Roll dimensions
roll_width(12).
roll_max_length(50).
1 | % Pieces to cut (piece_id, original_width, original_length)
piece(1, 6, 8).
piece(2, 4, 5).
piece(3, 5, 7).
piece(4, 8, 10).
2 | % Possible positions and orientations
% For each piece, we can place it in normal or rotated orientation
% placed(piece_id, x_pos, y_pos, width, height) - final placement
% rotation(piece_id, 0) means normal orientation, rotation(piece_id, 1) means rotated 90 degrees
3 | % Choice: Each piece must be placed exactly once with one rotation
1 { rotation(P, 0); rotation(P, 1) } 1 :- piece(P, _, _).
4 | % Derive actual dimensions based on rotation
actual_width(P, W) :- piece(P, W, _), rotation(P, 0).
actual_width(P, H) :- piece(P, _, H), rotation(P, 1).
actual_height(P, H) :- piece(P, _, H), rotation(P, 0).
actual_height(P, W) :- piece(P, W, _), rotation(P, 1).
5 | % Generate possible positions for each piece
% We'll use coordinates where (0,0) is bottom-left of roll
% x ranges from 0 to roll_width - piece_width
% y ranges from 0 to some reasonable maximum length
pos_x(0..11). % Since roll is 12ft wide, positions 0-11 are possible
pos_y(0..49). % Maximum length positions
6 | % Choice: Each piece must be placed at exactly one position
1 { placed(P, X, Y) : pos_x(X), pos_y(Y) } 1 :- piece(P, _, _).
7 | % Constraints: Pieces must fit within roll dimensions
:- placed(P, X, Y), actual_width(P, W), roll_width(RW), X + W > RW.
:- placed(P, X, Y), actual_height(P, H), roll_max_length(RL), Y + H > RL.
8 | % Non-overlap constraints: No two pieces can occupy the same space
:- placed(P1, X1, Y1), placed(P2, X2, Y2), P1 != P2,
   actual_width(P1, W1), actual_height(P1, H1),
   actual_width(P2, W2), actual_height(P2, H2),
   X1 < X2 + W2, X2 < X1 + W1,
   Y1 < Y2 + H2, Y2 < Y1 + H1.
9 | % Calculate the total length used
length_used(L) :- placed(P, X, Y), actual_height(P, H), L = Y + H.
10 | % Optimization: Minimize the maximum length used
#minimize { L : length_used(L) }.
